<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заволноваться.html>заволнова́ться</a> (10389)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заволочь.html>заволочь</a> (18455)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:волочь.html>воло́чь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">volóčʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заволочь.html>заволо́чь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavolóčʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заволакивать.html>завола́кивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to obscure, to cloud (the sun, the sky, one's eyes with tears, etc.)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:завораживать.html>завора́живать</a> (16829)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заворожить.html>заворожи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zavorožítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завораживать.html>завора́живать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavoráživatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заворожить.html>заворожи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cast a spell <i>(over)</i></li>
<li>to charm, to bewitch</li></ol>

***заворачивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заворачивать.html>завора́чивать</a> (11818)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">завороти́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zavorotítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заворачивать.html>завора́чивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavoráčivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завернуть.html>заверну́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">завороти́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to screw tight, to tighten
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заворачивать.html>завора́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кран.html>кран</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavoráčivatʹ</b> kran</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn off the tap</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to tuck up, to roll up</li>
<li>to wrap up <i>(in)</i></li>
<li>to turn
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заворачивать.html>завора́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:угол.html>у́гол</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavoráčivatʹ</b> za úgol</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn (round) the corner</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заворачивать.html>завора́чивай</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:отсюда.html>отсю́да</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavoráčivaj</b> otsjúda!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">turn back!; go away from here!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drop in <i>(at a place)</i>, to call <i>(at a place)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:заявление.html>заявле́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:завернуть.html>заверну́ли</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mojó zajavlénije zavernúli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">my application was turned down</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рукопись.html>ру́копись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:завернуть.html>заверну́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:издательство.html>изда́тельстве</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó rúkopisʹ zavernúli v izdátelʹstve</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he got a rejection slip from the publisher</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to begin, to come on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завернуть.html>заверну́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мороз.html>моро́зы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zavernúli morózy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">frosts came on</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to say, to utter, to let loose
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>ну</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:завернуть.html>заверну́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:речь.html>речь</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nu, ty i zavernúl rečʹ!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">some speech you made!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to run, to manage
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заворачивать.html>завора́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большими</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>дела́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zavoráčivatʹ</b> bolʹšimi delámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run a big business, be a big boss</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ра́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>чи<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — заворотить, <a href = vnd.unilang:завернуть.html>заверну́ть</a> (неправ. вм. завёртывать).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>за-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-ворач-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ива</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завывание.html>завыва́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavyvánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завывание.html>завыва́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завывание.html>завыва́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завывание.html>завыва́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> howling, howl</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> wailing, wail</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:завышенный.html>завы́шенный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zavýšennyj</span>)
